### Code Refactoring

- **api:** remove flat format support from request schemas ([67fb013](https://github.com/sovrium/sovrium/commit/67fb013c2ee3f3c33e9e07e11e2dd67b77be3a58))

Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.5 <noreply@anthropic.com>

- **specs:** Rollup and lookup field tests now expect computed values to be
  directly accessible as columns (Airtable-style), not manually computed via SQL.

## Problem

- Tests manually computed aggregations with JOIN/GROUP BY SQL
- Implementation burden on every query (performance cost)
- No single source of truth for computed field logic
- Tests validated SQL writing, not feature behavior

## Solution

- Tests now expect 'SELECT \* FROM table WHERE id = X' to return computed values
- Recommended implementation: PostgreSQL VIEWs (auto-recalculating)
- Tests validate behavior (values appear as columns) not implementation (SQL)
- Aligns with Airtable's model (computed fields are regular columns)

## Changes

- Rollup fields: All 11 tests redesigned (removed manual aggregations)
- Lookup fields: All 9 tests redesigned (removed manual JOINs)
- Added implementation guidance in test file headers
- Kept spec IDs unchanged (APP-TABLES-FIELD-TYPES-ROLLUP-XXX)
- All tests marked .fixme() for e2e-test-fixer implementation

## Implementation Approach (for e2e-test-fixer)

Use PostgreSQL VIEWs to provide Airtable-style computed columns:

Example for rollup:

```sql
CREATE VIEW customers_view AS
SELECT c.*, COALESCE(SUM(o.amount), 0) as total_order_amount
FROM customers c LEFT JOIN orders o ON c.id = o.customer_id GROUP BY c.id;
```

Example for lookup:

```sql
CREATE VIEW orders_view AS
SELECT o.*, c.name as customer_name, c.email as customer_email
FROM orders o LEFT JOIN customers c ON o.customer_id = c.id;
```

## Test Quality

- Zero errors (bun run analyze:specs)
- Clear acceptance criteria (GIVEN-WHEN-THEN)
- Realistic test data (no empty arrays)
- Behavioral assertions (test outcomes, not SQL)

* **auth:** `auth.authentication` renamed to `auth.methods`

🤖 Generated with [Claude Code](https://claude.com/claude-code)

- Complete rewrite of table specifications from UI/API testing to PostgreSQL database schema testing

## Changes

### Agent Documentation

- Updated `.claude/agents/json-schema-editor.md`:
  - Added "Database Testing Architecture" section
  - Documented testing separation: database (app/tables/) vs UI (app/pages/)
  - Added executeQuery fixture reference with usage examples
  - Documented field type → PostgreSQL type mapping table
  - Added quality gates for database testing
  - Provided correct/incorrect pattern examples

### Tables Schema Specifications

- Rewrote all 23 x-specs in `specs/app/tables/tables.schema.json`:
  - **Removed**: All UI testing (buttons, modals, forms, DOM, navigation)
  - **Removed**: All API testing without database validation
  - **Added**: PostgreSQL DDL validation using executeQuery
  - **Added**: Schema introspection queries (information_schema, pg_catalog)
  - **Added**: Constraint enforcement testing (UNIQUE, NOT NULL, CHECK, FOREIGN KEY)
  - **Added**: Data type mapping validation (JSON config → PostgreSQL types)

### New Spec Coverage

1. **APP-TABLES-SCHEMA-CREATE-001**: Table creation with DDL validation
2. **APP-TABLES-SCHEMA-FIELDS-001**: Multiple field type mapping
3. **APP-TABLES-SCHEMA-PK-001**: Primary key constraints
4. **APP-TABLES-SCHEMA-CONSTRAINTS-001**: UNIQUE, NOT NULL, CHECK constraints
5. **APP-TABLES-SCHEMA-INTROSPECT-001**: Schema introspection queries
6. **APP-TABLES-FIELD-TEXT-001**: VARCHAR column creation
7. **APP-TABLES-FIELD-EMAIL-001**: Email field with UNIQUE constraint
8. **APP-TABLES-FIELD-INTEGER-001**: INTEGER with CHECK constraints
9. **APP-TABLES-FIELD-DECIMAL-001**: NUMERIC type mapping
10. **APP-TABLES-FIELD-BOOLEAN-001**: BOOLEAN type mapping
11. **APP-TABLES-CONSTRAINT-UNIQUE-001**: UNIQUE constraint violation testing
12. **APP-TABLES-CONSTRAINT-NOT-NULL-001**: NOT NULL constraint testing
13. **APP-TABLES-CONSTRAINT-CHECK-001**: CHECK constraint range validation
14. **APP-TABLES-INDEX-CREATE-001**: Index creation and pg_indexes validation
15. **APP-TABLES-MIGRATION-ALTER-001**: ALTER TABLE ADD COLUMN migration
16. **APP-TABLES-MIGRATION-DROP-001**: ALTER TABLE DROP COLUMN migration
17. **APP-TABLES-DATA-INSERT-001**: INSERT with RETURNING clause
18. **APP-TABLES-DATA-UPDATE-001**: UPDATE statement validation
19. **APP-TABLES-DATA-DELETE-001**: DELETE statement validation
20. **APP-TABLES-FIELD-TIMESTAMP-001**: TIMESTAMP with DEFAULT NOW()
21. **APP-TABLES-FIELD-SELECT-001**: Single-select with CHECK constraint
22. **APP-TABLES-DROP-001**: DROP TABLE validation
23. **APP-TABLES-COMPOSITE-PK-001**: Composite primary key

## Impact

This architectural shift ensures:

- ✅ App tables specs test PostgreSQL schema generation (correct focus)
- ✅ Zero UI references in database testing specs (separation of concerns)
- ✅ All specs use executeQuery fixture for direct database operations
- ✅ Specs validate configuration → DDL transformation
- ✅ Proper test separation: app/tables/ (DB) vs app/pages/ (UI)

## Related

- Follows guidance from product-specs-architect agent review
- Aligns with database testing architecture documented in json-schema-editor.md
- Part of Phase 1 & 2 of specification quality improvement roadmap

- Remove {{key}} pattern entirely - use ONLY $t:key pattern

Changes:

- Remove ALL {{}} pattern handling from translation-replacer.ts
- Use $t:key pattern exclusively for both dynamic SSR and static SSG
- Set meta.lang programmatically (full locale) instead of via token
- Migrate static-i18n.spec.ts: ~30 occurrences {{key}} → $t:key
- Migrate static-deployment.spec.ts: ~10 occurrences {{key}} → $t:key
- Fix STATIC-I18N-003 test expectations to match correct implementation:
  - Use full locales in hreflang (en-US not en) for SEO best practice
  - Use relative URLs (/en/) not absolute URLs
  - Include trailing slashes in paths (/en/about/)

Rationale:

- Single source of truth for translation resolution
- Same app config works for both dynamic and static deployment
- Consistent translation fallback behavior across contexts
- No backward compatibility maintained per user request

Implementation:

- translation-replacer.ts now uses resolveTranslation() for $t: patterns
- Leverages centralized translation resolution with fallback support
- meta.lang set to langConfig.locale || langCode programmatically

Validation:

- All unit tests passing (2349 tests)
- All static E2E tests passing (14/14 implemented tests)
- Pattern unified across entire codebase

Co-Authored-By: Claude <noreply@anthropic.com>

- Happy DOM is no longer globally preloaded for all tests

**Problem**: Happy DOM's global registration was interfering with server-side tests:

- API schema diff tests failing with "Invalid URL" in @apidevtools/json-schema-ref-parser
- Auth routes tests failing with "Invalid base URL" in Better Auth
- Happy DOM's global URL override broke URL resolution in 15 tests

**Solution**:

- Removed global preload from bunfig.toml
- Updated happydom.ts to be imported per test file (not global)
- Updated RTL documentation with correct import pattern
- Existing React tests use SSR (renderToString) and don't need DOM

**Test Results**:

- Before: 1857 pass, 15 fail
- After: 1889 pass, 0 fail

**Usage**: Import './happydom' in React component tests that need DOM APIs
(RTL + interactive component testing). Server-side tests (SSR, API, schema)
don't need DOM and should NOT import it.

- Theme CSS is now compiled globally at server startup via CSS compiler instead of per-page runtime generation.

Changes:

- Update CSS compiler to accept app parameter and generate Tailwind @theme CSS
- Create theme-to-CSS conversion helpers (colors, fonts, spacing, shadows, border-radius, breakpoints, animations)

- Remove runtime theme CSS generation from DynamicPage and PageHead
- Delete entire presentation/theming/ directory (theme generators no longer needed)
- Theme is still passed to components for font URLs, animation flags, and debugging
- CSS is now served from global /assets/output.css with compiled theme tokens

Benefits:

- Single source of truth: app.theme → Tailwind @theme
- Better performance: Compile once at startup (not per-page)
- Simpler architecture: Remove duplicate CSS generation layer
- Global consistency: One theme across all pages
- Standard Tailwind: Use standard Tailwind utilities (bg-primary, text-secondary)

Co-Authored-By: Claude <noreply@anthropic.com>

- Per-component i18n removed entirely in favor of pure centralized translations

**Rationale:**

- Industry standards (i18next, vue-i18n, react-intl, next-intl) use pure centralized i18n
- Per-component overrides create maintenance burden and translation duplication
- Centralized pattern provides single source of truth
- Simpler mental model: 100% of translations in one place

**Files Deleted:**

1. specs/app/pages/common/i18n.schema.json (deprecated schema)
2. specs/app/pages/common/i18n.spec.ts (redundant tests - covered by languages.spec.ts)

**Schema Changes:**

1. specs/app/pages/sections/sections.schema.json:
   - Removed i18n property from section component definition
   - Deleted APP-PAGES-SECTIONS-008 spec (tested per-component i18n)
   - Updated APP-PAGES-SECTIONS-012 spec:
     - Changed from "all 3 optional properties" to "multiple optional properties"
     - Removed i18n from validation and application examples
     - Now tests interactions + responsive only (not i18n)

**Test Changes:**

1. specs/app/pages/sections/sections.spec.ts:
   - Removed APP-PAGES-SECTIONS-008 test (per-component i18n)
   - Updated APP-PAGES-SECTIONS-012 test title and removed i18n property

**Impact:**

- Schemas: 324 → 323 (i18n.schema.json deleted)
- Specs: 1720 → 1718 (2 per-component i18n specs removed)
- Validation: 0 errors

**Migration Path:**
All translations now MUST use centralized pattern:

```json
{
  "languages": {
    "translations": {
      "en-US": {
        "button.save": "Save",
        "forms.email.placeholder": "Enter email"
      },
      "fr-FR": {
        "button.save": "Enregistrer",
        "forms.email.placeholder": "Entrez votre e-mail"
      }
    }
  },
  "sections": [
    { "type": "button", "children": ["$t:button.save"] },
    { "type": "input", "props": { "placeholder": "$t:forms.email.placeholder" } }
  ]
}
```

**For context-specific text**, use specific translation keys:

- ❌ Old (removed): Per-component override with generic key
- ✅ New (required): Specific centralized keys (payment.submit, form.submit)

**Benefits:**

- Single source of truth for ALL translations
- No precedence rules to remember
- Easier to audit missing translations
- Better translator workflow (one file to translate)
- Consistent with industry standards

🤖 Generated with [Claude Code](https://claude.com/claude-code)

Co-Authored-By: Claude <noreply@anthropic.com>

- **i18n:** (v0.2.0): Per-component i18n will be removed in v0.2.0

**Rationale:**

- Industry standards (i18next, vue-i18n, react-intl, next-intl) use pure centralized i18n
- Per-component overrides create translation duplication and maintenance burden
- Centralized pattern provides single source of truth for all translations

**Changes:**

1. **Deprecated per-component i18n** (specs/app/pages/common/i18n.schema.json):
   - Marked schema as DEPRECATED with migration instructions
   - Added deprecation warning to description
   - Removed 11 x-specs (APP-I18N-001 through 010, 012) testing deprecated pattern
   - Kept only APP-I18N-011 (tests centralized $t: pattern)

2. **Refactored i18n tests** (specs/app/pages/common/i18n.spec.ts):
   - Removed all per-component i18n tests (11 tests deleted)
   - Kept APP-I18N-011 (centralized pattern test)
   - Added comprehensive regression test showing $t: in multiple prop types

3. **Enhanced centralized pattern** (specs/app/languages/languages.schema.json):
   - Updated description: $t: works in ANY string property (not just children)
   - Added translation keys for accessibility (a11y._) and images (images._.alt)
   - Added comprehensive example showing $t: in children, props, meta
   - Improved translation key conventions documentation
   - Removed APP-LANGUAGES-017 (hybrid precedence test)

4. **Updated documentation** (docs/architecture/patterns/i18n-centralized-translations.md):
   - Removed "FALLBACK: Per-Component i18n" section
   - Removed "Translation Resolution (Precedence Order)" section
   - Removed hybrid examples and precedence rules
   - Updated migration guide for v0.1.x → v0.2.0
   - Clarified: 100% centralized, 0% per-component

5. **Added deprecation warnings** (scripts/validate-app-specs.ts):
   - Added validateDeprecatedI18n() function
   - Emits warnings when per-component i18n detected in schemas
   - Skips examples/x-specs (they're documentation)
   - Provides migration path in warning message

6. **Removed hybrid test** (specs/app/languages/languages.spec.ts):
   - Deleted APP-LANGUAGES-017 test (per-component override precedence)

**Migration Path:**

v0.1.1 (current): Deprecation warnings emitted
v0.2.0: Per-component i18n removed entirely

**For context-specific text**, use specific translation keys:

- ❌ Bad: `common.submit` with per-component override
- ✅ Good: `payment.submit`, `form.submit` (specific centralized keys)

**Pattern examples:**

```json
{
  "translations": {
    "en-US": {
      "button.save": "Save",
      "forms.email.placeholder": "Enter email",
      "a11y.close": "Close",
      "images.logo.alt": "Company logo"
    }
  },
  "components": [
    { "type": "button", "children": ["$t:button.save"] },
    { "type": "input", "props": { "placeholder": "$t:forms.email.placeholder" } },
    { "type": "button", "props": { "aria-label": "$t:a11y.close" } },
    { "type": "img", "props": { "alt": "$t:images.logo.alt" } }
  ]
}
```

**Validation:**

- 0 errors (schemas validate correctly)
- Total specs: 1732 → 1720 (12 deprecated specs removed)

Before:

- kebab-case for 9 file types
- PascalCase for use cases, ports, repositories, errors, page components
- Mixed conventions increased cognitive load

After:

- kebab-case for 95% of files (default)
- PascalCase ONLY for page-level components (5%)

Key improvements:

- Simpler mental model: "kebab-case unless it's a page"
- File ≠ export principle: start-server.ts exports startServer
- Ecosystem aligned: matches URLs, CLI tools, React hooks, shadcn/ui
- Minimal decision fatigue: one default style
- Quick decision tree: "Is it a page? → PascalCase, else → kebab-case"

Affected conventions:

- Use cases: StartServer.ts → start-server.ts
- Ports: IConfigLoader.ts → config-loader.ts or i-config-loader.ts
- Repositories: UserRepository.ts → user-repository.ts
- Errors: InvalidConfigError.ts → invalid-config-error.ts
- Layers: AppLayer.ts → app-layer.ts

Page components remain PascalCase: DefaultHomePage.tsx ✓
